Root cause: `@cloudflare/containers@0.3.6` mounts the ephemeral containers CA at `/etc/cloudflare/certs/` only once HTTPS interception is registered, and the SDK deliberately registers it ahead of `container.start()` so the cert exists when the container entrypoint installs it into the trust store. codeflare wired `interceptOutboundHttps` in `onStart` — which fires *after* the container has booted and `entrypoint.sh` has already run its CA-trust block ([REQ-ENTERPRISE-005](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-005-container-side-enterprise-routing-ca-trust--constant-base-urls) AC2) — so the entrypoint found no cert, skipped trust, and every agent's intercepted-TLS handshake to `api.openai.com` failed at the connection layer (the interceptor was never reached and the gateway logs stayed empty, looking like a broken gateway). Fix: `setupEnterpriseInterception` moves out of `onStart` into a `startAndWaitForPorts` override that wires interception before `super.startAndWaitForPorts()` (= before the SDK's `container.start()`), mirroring where the SDK applies its own pre-start interception; all start paths (explicit start + `containerFetch` auto-start) funnel through it. Flag-unset parity preserved: the override is a no-op when `ENTERPRISE_MODE` is unset, so the SaaS start path is byte-identical. Status stays Planned (`index.test.ts` enterprise-interception-wiring describe asserts the pre-start ordering + the non-enterprise no-op).

## 2026-06-05

- **REQ-ENTERPRISE-004 split** to honour the 7-AC cap (per user direction, PR #499): the gateway route-pinning AC is extracted into a new [REQ-ENTERPRISE-007](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-007-gateway-route-pinning) (Gateway Route-Pinning, 2 ACs), returning [REQ-ENTERPRISE-004](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-004-outbound-interception-llm-routing-to-customer-ai-gateway) to 7 ACs. The `llm-interceptor.test.ts` route-pinning describe is renamed to REQ-ENTERPRISE-007 and the inline cross-refs in [REQ-ENTERPRISE-005](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-005-container-side-enterprise-routing-ca-trust--constant-base-urls) AC3 and [REQ-ENTERPRISE-006](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-006-deploy-time-aig-secrets-and-enterprise_mode-var) AC2 are repointed to REQ-ENTERPRISE-007. No behaviour change.
- Enterprise gateway route-pinning moved to the **Worker interceptor**; the `AIG_LANGUAGE_MODEL` → container fan-out (added earlier today, the entry below) is **reverted** ([REQ-ENTERPRISE-004](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-004-outbound-interception-llm-routing-to-customer-ai-gateway) route-pinning AC added, later split to [REQ-ENTERPRISE-007](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-007-gateway-route-pinning); [REQ-ENTERPRISE-005](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-005-container-side-enterprise-routing-ca-trust--constant-base-urls) AC1/AC3/AC5; [REQ-ENTERPRISE-006](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-006-deploy-time-aig-secrets-and-enterprise_mode-var) AC2; [AD74](../../documentation/decisions/README.md#ad74-enterprise-llm-transport-on-the-ai-gateway-rest-api) route-pinning amendment). Root cause from a live enterprise deploy: a gateway dynamic route is invoked by `model: dynamic/<route>`, but Pi parses a slash in a model id as `provider/model` and bound `dynamic/codeflare-enterprise` to its built-in amazon-bedrock provider (falsely "authenticated" by the container's R2 S3 keys, exported under the generic `AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID`/`AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY` names), signing a SigV4 call that never reached `api.openai.com` — empty gateway logs, looking like a broken Worker route. Fix: (1) `AIG_LANGUAGE_MODEL` is now **Worker-only** — `buildEnvVars` no longer fans it into the container as `COPILOT_MODEL`/`PI_MODEL`; (2) `LlmInterceptor` rewrites the request `model` to `AIG_LANGUAGE_MODEL` on egress for `/chat/completions` + `/responses` (route-pinning; non-JSON / model-less bodies pass through, response stays zero-copy) — so agents carry only a fixed slash-free handle (`codeflare`) and the route name never enters the container; (3) `entrypoint.sh` configures Copilot with the complete BYOK 3-var contract (keeping `GH_TOKEN` for GitHub-hosted features; `COPILOT_OFFLINE=true` documented as the deterministic fallback) and pins Pi via `~/.pi/agent/settings.json` `defaultProvider`/`defaultModel` so it is gateway-bound zero-touch instead of auto-selecting a built-in. AD74's "no model rewrite / zero-copy passthrough" claim is narrowed accordingly (response zero-copy; request `model` field substituted). Flag-unset parity preserved (interceptor never instantiated, no enterprise container vars).
- Enterprise environment is now deployable from any branch (e.g. `develop`) via the `deploy.yml` workflow_dispatch `target=enterprise`, not only from `main`, so enterprise can be iterated without a merge-to-main round-trip. `production` stays locked to `main` (the existing guard step is unchanged); a non-main, non-enterprise dispatch still maps to `integration`. The GitHub `enterprise` environment's deployment-branch policy is widened to allow `develop` alongside `main`. ([REQ-ENTERPRISE-006](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-006-deploy-time-aig-secrets-and-enterprise_mode-var) deploy plumbing.)
- Enterprise LLM transport migrated off the **deprecated** AI Gateway paths onto the **REST API**, and **Claude Code dropped from the enterprise agent set** ([REQ-ENTERPRISE-003](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-003-agent-allowlist-in-enterprise-mode), [REQ-ENTERPRISE-004](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-004-outbound-interception-llm-routing-to-customer-ai-gateway), [REQ-ENTERPRISE-005](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-005-container-side-enterprise-routing-ca-trust--constant-base-urls), [REQ-ENTERPRISE-006](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-006-deploy-time-aig-secrets-and-enterprise_mode-var); [AD74](../../documentation/decisions/README.md#ad74-enterprise-llm-transport-on-the-ai-gateway-rest-api)). The original 2026-06-04 design forwarded intercepted traffic to `gateway.ai.cloudflare.com/v1/{acct}/{gw}/compat` and `/anthropic` with a `cf-aig-authorization` header — both paths Cloudflare has since deprecated ("continue to work for existing integrations"). A live smoke test against the `codeflare-enterprise` gateway confirmed the recommended REST API at `api.cloudflare.com/client/v4/accounts/{account_id}/ai/v1/*` carries everything the transport needs (dynamic routing via `model: "dynamic/<route>"`, SSE streaming, `cf-aig-metadata` attribution, BYOK + Workers AI), so [REQ-ENTERPRISE-004](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-004-outbound-interception-llm-routing-to-customer-ai-gateway) now maps the intercepted host onto `https://api.cloudflare.com/client/v4/accounts/{account_id}/ai/v1/<path>`, authenticates with the standard `Authorization: Bearer <AIG_TOKEN>` header (the same token, moved off `cf-aig-authorization`), and routes with `cf-aig-gateway-id`. The account id and gateway id are parsed from the existing `AIG_GATEWAY_URL` secret ([REQ-ENTERPRISE-006](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-006-deploy-time-aig-secrets-and-enterprise_mode-var) AC4 fails closed 503 when it is unset **or unparseable**); no new secret or binding. The interception **mechanism** from [AD72](../../documentation/decisions/README.md#ad72-outbound-https-interception-over-a-worker-side-llm-proxy-for-enterprise-gateway-routing) is unchanged — only the upstream target, auth header, and agent set change. The REST API's Anthropic-compatible endpoint requires author-prefixed model ids (`anthropic/claude-…`) while Claude Code emits a bare `claude-…` model, which would force a per-request body rewrite and break the zero-copy passthrough; rather than carry that, Claude Code is removed from the enterprise roster ([REQ-ENTERPRISE-003](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-003-agent-allowlist-in-enterprise-mode) AC1 now `{copilot, pi, bash}`, mirrored in `agent-allowlist.ts` and `CreateSessionDialog.tsx`). With only OpenAI-wire-format agents left, the interceptor forwards the body unchanged and intercepts only `api.openai.com` ([REQ-ENTERPRISE-004](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-004-outbound-interception-llm-routing-to-customer-ai-gateway) AC6: `api.anthropic.com` now 400). Backend selection (native provider, Amazon Bedrock, Workers AI, or a dynamic route with rate-limit/budget/fallback) is entirely gateway-side via each agent's configured model id; codeflare holds no provider keys (BYOK lives in the gateway). [REQ-ENTERPRISE-005](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-005-container-side-enterprise-routing-ca-trust--constant-base-urls) AC3 drops the Claude `ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL`/`ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN` injection (Claude Code no longer launches in enterprise); Anthropic models remain reachable via Copilot/Pi by model id. Flag-unset parity is preserved end-to-end: `ENTERPRISE_MODE` unset ⇒ the interceptor is never instantiated and non-enterprise behaviour is byte-identical.
- [REQ-ENTERPRISE-001](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-001-enterprise_mode-forces-unlimited-tier-and-pro-mode) AC3 tightened: every enterprise user is explicitly a custom `unlimited` user whose monthly compute quota (timekeeper) is never enforced and whose session cap is the unlimited tier's cap — "no time limit" language now matches the implemented and tested behaviour in `container-lifecycle-helpers.test.ts`. `Applies To` corrected from Admin to User (the AC governs runtime enforcement for every user, not the deployer who sets the flag).
- Browser Run reworked from the original "chrome-devtools-mcp for all MCP-capable agents" design to **per-agent-by-capability**, because Pi does not consume MCP servers (native tools ship as `pi.registerTool` extensions like the first-party `graphify-native.ts`). [REQ-BROWSER-001](browser-run.md#req-browser-001-browser-run-as-a-webfetch-fallback-claude-code-via-chrome-devtools-mcp) now scopes the `chrome-devtools-mcp` (CDP) path to **Claude Code**, wired in `entrypoint.sh` behind the advanced-mode + Cloudflare-token gate plus a seeded `browser-run` skill. [REQ-BROWSER-003](browser-run.md#req-browser-003-pi-native-browser-run-wrapper) is rewritten as a **Pi native wrapper**: a `preseed/agents/pi/extensions/browser-run.ts` extension registering `browser_markdown` / `browser_content` / `browser_scrape` tools over the Browser Run REST Quick Actions (`/markdown`, `/content`, `/scrape`), self-gated on the Cloudflare token, seeded advanced-mode-only and baked into `src/lib/agent-seed.generated.ts`. **GitHub Copilot wiring is deferred** (removed from this iteration's scope and the entrypoint). REQ-BROWSER-001 and REQ-BROWSER-003 move Planned→Partial (built + gated; runtime/preseed artifacts with no Worker-suite unit test). [REQ-BROWSER-002](browser-run.md#req-browser-002-browser-rendering-scope-in-the-cloudflare-token-template) (the `Browser Rendering - Edit` token scope) moves Planned→Implemented (scope present + `token-scopes.test.ts`).

## 2026-06-04

- New domain [Enterprise Mode](enterprise-mode.md) added (`spec/enterprise-mode.md`, [REQ-ENTERPRISE-001](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-001-enterprise_mode-forces-unlimited-tier-and-pro-mode)..[REQ-ENTERPRISE-006](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-006-deploy-time-aig-secrets-and-enterprise_mode-var), all Planned): a deploy-time `ENTERPRISE_MODE` Worker var turns a deployment into a single-tenant enterprise instance. [REQ-ENTERPRISE-001](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-001-enterprise_mode-forces-unlimited-tier-and-pro-mode) forces every user to the `unlimited` tier in Pro (advanced) mode and disables subscription enforcement (quota/billing/trial) — CRITICAL flag-unset parity: when the flag is unset, tier/mode/subscription resolution is byte-identical to today across the Default/Onboarding/SaaS deployment modes ([REQ-SUB-001](subscription.md#req-sub-001-eight-tier-subscription-system), [REQ-SUB-014](subscription.md#req-sub-014-session-mode-gating-by-tier), [REQ-AGENT-004](agents.md#req-agent-004-two-session-modes-standard-and-pro), [REQ-SETUP-003](setup.md#req-setup-003-three-deployment-modes)). [REQ-ENTERPRISE-002](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-002-subscription-ui-hidden-and-subscribe-route-guarded) hides the billing UI and guards `/app/subscribe`; [REQ-ENTERPRISE-003](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-003-agent-allowlist-in-enterprise-mode) narrows the agent roster to `{claude-code, copilot, pi, bash}` (all seven when the flag is unset, per [REQ-AGENT-001](agents.md#req-agent-001-support-multiple-ai-coding-agents)); [REQ-ENTERPRISE-004](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-004-outbound-interception-llm-routing-to-customer-ai-gateway) routes agent LLM traffic to the customer's AI Gateway via platform outbound-HTTPS interception: the container DO wires `ctx.container.interceptOutboundHttps` + `ctx.exports` (both on by default at this project's compat date — the `enable_ctx_exports` flag became the default on 2025-11-17, so no flag is set) so the container's HTTPS to the real provider hosts (`api.anthropic.com`/`api.openai.com`) is routed at the platform level to an `LlmInterceptor` `WorkerEntrypoint` holding the gateway URL+token in its Worker env (never in the container, never a public route, so never behind Cloudflare Access), maps each onto the gateway provider path, stamps `cf-aig-authorization` + `cf-aig-metadata` with an opaque per-user id (a per-session DO prop), strips the container's placeholder auth, preserves streaming, and fails closed on an unmapped host (400) or unconfigured gateway (503); [REQ-ENTERPRISE-005](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-005-container-side-enterprise-routing-ca-trust--constant-base-urls) is the container-side half — `buildEnvVars` emits only the `ENTERPRISE_MODE` flag (no per-session URL/token), and entrypoint.sh installs the Cloudflare containers CA so the intercepted TLS validates and points each agent at the constant real provider base-URL with a non-secret placeholder credential (Claude `ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL`/`ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN`, Copilot BYOK, Pi `models.json`; [REQ-AGENT-031](agents.md#req-agent-031-consult-llm-key-isolation-subscription-backend-and-multi-agent-parity)); [REQ-ENTERPRISE-006](enterprise-mode.md#req-enterprise-006-deploy-time-aig-secrets-and-enterprise_mode-var) defines the deploy-time plumbing (`AIG_GATEWAY_URL` + `AIG_TOKEN` as Worker secrets, `ENTERPRISE_MODE` as a var, off by default).
- New domain [Browser Run](browser-run.md) added (`spec/browser-run.md`, [REQ-BROWSER-001](browser-run.md#req-browser-001-browser-run-as-a-webfetch-fallback-claude-code-via-chrome-devtools-mcp)..[REQ-BROWSER-003](browser-run.md#req-browser-003-pi-native-browser-run-wrapper), all Planned): a real-browser WebFetch fallback backed by Cloudflare Browser Run. [REQ-BROWSER-001](browser-run.md#req-browser-001-browser-run-as-a-webfetch-fallback-claude-code-via-chrome-devtools-mcp) registers chrome-devtools-mcp in Pro (advanced) mode only, pointed at the Browser Run CDP `/devtools` endpoint, giving the agent a real browser to retry public targets when WebFetch is blocked (bot protection, login walls, redirect chains, JS-only pages) — public targets only, no e2e, no in-browser code-execution sandbox; [REQ-BROWSER-002](browser-run.md#req-browser-002-browser-rendering-scope-in-the-cloudflare-token-template) adds the `Browser Rendering - Edit` scope to the user-pasted Cloudflare token template (additive; existing tokens keep working, per [REQ-AGENT-010](agents.md#req-agent-010-deploy-credential-storage-github-pat-cf-api-token)); [REQ-BROWSER-003](browser-run.md#req-browser-003-pi-native-browser-run-wrapper) wires chrome-devtools-mcp for MCP-capable agents (Claude and Copilot natively, Pi via its `mcp.json` bridge) through the existing adaptation pipeline ([REQ-AGENT-007](agents.md#req-agent-007-multi-agent-adaptation-pipeline)).
- [REQ-SESSION-011](session-lifecycle.md#req-session-011-graceful-shutdown-with-final-sync) reworked: every deliberate stop (user stop, delete, idle timeout, quota eviction) now awaits a live R2 bisync to completion before the container is signalled to stop, so edits made in the seconds before shutdown reach R2 instead of being cut off by the platform's ~3s SIGKILL window that the old SIGTERM-trap final sync relied on. Full root-cause and mechanism (awaitable `/internal/final-sync` endpoint, 120s drain budget, 135s teardown cap, trap-as-backstop) are in [AD57](../../documentation/decisions/README.md#ad57-135-second-shutdown-budget-for-final-bisync).
- [REQ-SESSION-018](session-lifecycle.md#req-session-018-persisted-status-is-authoritative-on-container-exit) AC3+AC4 added (false-stopped hardening; observed live on a long-running production Pi session shown stopped on the dashboard for ~14 minutes while actually running). Root cause was two compounding gaps left by the 2026-06-02 split: (1) `onError` still wrote `stopped` immediately on a single `!ctx.container.running` reading - the same transient false reading AC2 hardened the `collectMetrics` catch-all against - so a spurious "Container error" (deploy-roll / monitor blip) flipped a live container to stopped; and (2) once KV read stopped, the `collectMetrics` clobber-race guard refused every subsequent write, so the alarm loop watched the container stay alive for 14 minutes without ever correcting the status (recovery only came on a real restart). AC3: `onError` no longer writes stopped on a not-running reading - it opens the existing not-running confirmation window (`openNotRunningConfirmation`) and re-arms a `collectMetrics` tick, delegating the stopped decision to that window (a genuine crash confirms to stopped within the window; a recovered container clears it with no false stopped). The cost is `onError` latency: a real crash now transitions after the window (one to a few ticks) rather than immediately - accepted because a live session shown stopped strands the user while a crashed session shown running self-corrects. AC4: `collectMetrics` self-heals - when the container is demonstrably running (running branch reached after a successful `/health` probe) but KV reads stopped, it re-asserts running, bounding any false-stopped to a single alarm tick; it does not resurrect a deliberate stop. The deliberate-stop guard is a PERSISTED DO-storage marker (`shutdownRequested`) that `destroy()` writes as its first action - before clearing identifiers - and also drops the metrics alarm; `onStart()` clears it on the next start. It is persisted rather than an in-memory field for the same reason the not-running window is (per the code-reviewer's finding on PR #493): a DO eviction mid-shutdown would reset an in-memory flag to 0, and the surviving alarm would then resurrect a session the user just stopped; the persisted marker survives that eviction. The stale canonical lifecycle-contract comment in `src/container/index.ts` (which still asserted "onError MUST write 'stopped'") is corrected to describe the window-deferral. Accepted tradeoff (documented in Constraints): crash-to-stopped convergence now depends on DO alarm delivery waking the DO to run the re-armed tick, the same dependency the catch-all already has. Behavior fix; no removal.
- [REQ-STOR-011](storage.md#req-stor-011-sync-mode-controls-workspace-scope) / [REQ-MEM-009](memory.md#req-mem-009-vault-graph-accumulates-monotonically-across-extractions): R2 bisync now excludes derived `Vault/graphify-out/` files (per-run graph.json, chunks, labels, GRAPH_REPORT.md, cache/, manifest.json) and `.codex/skills/.system/**` (Codex's binary-bundled system skills, re-extracted on launch); `vault-graph.json` and `graph.html` are explicitly re-included ahead of the blanket exclude so the cumulative vault graph persists. Excludes regenerable/derived content with no R2 restore value; no AC change.
- [REQ-OPS-003](operations.md#req-ops-003-pr-checks-run-lint-test-typecheck-and-security-audit): PR Checks may accept the known Cloudflare Workers-pool shutdown crash only after retry and only when the backend test log proves the expected complete suite passed with no failed-test tokens; incomplete backend runs and assertion failures still fail the workflow.
- [REQ-AGENT-053](agents.md#req-agent-053-pi-durable-review-status-and-result-formatting): Pi durable review finalization now recovers from persisted exact-head result files during passive refresh, so missed lane-completion callbacks or reloads still finalize, acknowledge, and publish the merged review once every required result file exists.
- [REQ-AGENT-056](agents.md#req-agent-056-pi-local-statusline-footer): Pi local statusline now repaints on a cache-TTL interval because custom footers can read `footerData.getExtensionStatuses()` but Pi does not expose a status-change subscription; review status rows therefore refresh as extension-owned statuses change.
- [REQ-AGENT-056](agents.md#req-agent-056-pi-local-statusline-footer): Pi local statusline truncation now counts visible characters only, preserves ANSI color sequences in extension-owned review status rows, and resets styling before the ellipsis so colored lane labels do not shorten the visible footer or bleed color after truncation.
- [REQ-AGENT-059](agents.md#req-agent-059-pi-durable-review-fix-loop): Pi review autofix is requested only after the exact-head durable review job is complete and every required lane has a result file; partial lane results cannot trigger edit/commit/push follow-ups. The hidden autofix prompt now also explicitly forbids fixing from partial lane results.
- [REQ-AGENT-036](agents.md#req-agent-036-pr-boundary-review-trigger-conditions) / [REQ-AGENT-054](agents.md#req-agent-054-pi-durable-review-lane-failure-handling) / [REQ-AGENT-056](agents.md#req-agent-056-pi-local-statusline-footer): Pi review detection now resolves command-local `cd` prefixes separated by `&&`, semicolon, or newline; durable review retry suppression uses in-memory active lanes only, and the Pi local statusline is preseeded for both Standard and Pro while preserving review progress statuses.
- [REQ-MEM-009](memory.md#req-mem-009-vault-graph-accumulates-monotonically-across-extractions) / [REQ-MEM-001](memory.md#req-mem-001-conversation-context-automatically-captured-to-vault) / [REQ-VAULT-016](vault.md#req-vault-016-vault-graph-extraction-emits-the-canonical-shared-schema): Pi memory/vault graph brought to full parity with Claude - all four pipelines (vault-extract + memory-capture, both runtimes) now converge on a single cumulative `vault-graph.json` built by the shared `merge-vault-graph.py` and publish that cumulative graph to the global graph as `user_vault`. Three defects fixed: (1) Claude memory-capture (and both Pi pipelines) previously built a throwaway per-chunk `graph.json` and ran `graphify global add graph.json --as user_vault`, whose replace-semantics wiped all prior vault knowledge on every run; they now run `merge-vault-graph.py` (load cumulative `vault-graph.json`, `nx.compose` the chunk, re-cluster, persist) and global-add the cumulative `vault-graph.json`. (2) Pi was self-reliant on no `.claude` path: `merge-vault-graph.py` now ships its own copy under `preseed/agents/pi/scripts/`, registered in the Pi manifest and deployed byte-identical to `/home/user/.pi/agent/scripts/` so Pi never reaches into the Claude plugin tree. (3) The Pi `memory-vault.ts` in-process deterministic baseline (`deterministicVaultGraph`/`stableId`/`titleFor`) is removed - it maintained a competing `graph.json` store the canonical merge overwrote; the extension is now a pure trigger and the vault-extract subagent authors the structural nodes via the chunk exactly like Claude. REQ-MEM-009 `@impl` scope expands to all four pipelines; REQ-MEM-001 AC6 moves off inline `build_from_json`/`cluster`/`to_json`; REQ-VAULT-016 AC1 drops the extension-baseline clause (both runtimes' subagents emit the schema). The robustness floor (a guaranteed no-LLM pass) is traded for exact Claude parity; the Pi subagent spawn has a `sendUserMessage` fallback.
- [REQ-VAULT-003](vault.md#req-vault-003-user-curated-edits-are-detected-and-ingested-within-60s): fixed a Pi-only deadlock that stopped the vault-extract trigger from ever firing under Pi. The entrypoint `start_vault_monitor_daemon` is gated on `SESSION_MODE=advanced`, not on runtime, so it runs under Pi too and writes the shared-namespace `~/.cache/codeflare-hooks/vault-extract.vars` on any vault change. Under Claude its UserPromptSubmit hook consumes that file; under Pi nothing does, and the Pi `memory-vault.ts` extension read the SAME path as its own pending sentinel - so `vaultVarsPending()` returned true forever and `agent_end` bailed before it could detect the edit or spawn the subagent (observed live on integration: a daemon-written `.vars` at 14:33 blocked a note edited at 14:34, same container boot). The two detectors shared one sentinel with incompatible producer/consumer wiring. Fix: the Pi extension now owns runtime-namespaced sentinels (`vault-extract.pi.vars` / `vault-extract.pi.in-flight`) and shares only the `vault-extract.last` high-water marker - advancing `.last` each turn makes the daemon's own `find -newer` come up empty, so the daemon stays quiet instead of fighting Pi. `vaultVarsPending()` also self-heals a `.pi.vars` left by a crashed subagent once it ages past the in-flight TTL, and the Pi vault-extract prompt removes the in-flight file by its `inflightFile` vars value rather than a hard-coded name. `.cache/**` is already excluded from R2 bisync (entrypoint.sh), so these sentinels were always session-local; the bug was an intra-session collision, not cross-session persistence. Behavior-only fix; no AC change.
- [REQ-AGENT-025](agents.md#req-agent-025-post-clone-graph-triage) / [REQ-AGENT-043](agents.md#req-agent-043-graphify-build-mode-dispatch): post-clone graph triage no longer tells agents to refresh stale existing graphs automatically. Missing-graph prompts now offer Full repo AST-only, Full repo semantic, or no graph action. Existing stale/unknown graph prompts now ask before any update, offering existing-graph-as-is, Full repo AST-only update, or Full repo semantic refresh. A same-turn clone-time AST/Full choice counts as the graphify skill's mode choice after detection, so the user is not asked the same AST/Full question twice.

## 2026-06-02

- [REQ-SESSION-018](session-lifecycle.md#req-session-018-persisted-status-is-authoritative-on-container-exit) added (write-side authority, split from [REQ-SESSION-010](session-lifecycle.md#req-session-010-session-status-observable-from-dashboard)); the read-side `reconcileStaleStatus` heuristic (introduced 2026-05-31 for the dangling-running issue, codeflare#153) is removed. KV `status` is now authoritative: a container that exits for any reason - graceful stop, crash, or an unexpected exit the SDK surfaces as `onError` - writes `stopped` to KV (the `collectMetrics` not-running branch + `onError`), so the dashboard reflects reality directly from the list metadata. The previous heuristic downgraded a `running` session to `stopped` whenever its metrics heartbeat (`m.u`) was older than 5 minutes; because the heartbeat freezes when the collectMetrics alarm loop dies on an unexpected exit, it falsely kicked users off still-live sessions while never fixing the underlying missing-write (the exit path wrote nothing to KV, so the record dangled `running`). Removing it eliminates the false kick; the exit-writes-stopped contract eliminates the dangling record. `reconcileStaleStatus` + `STALE_RUNNING_MS` and all five call sites (`session/lifecycle.ts` batch-status, `session/crud.ts` session list, `container/lifecycle.ts` session-limit counter) are deleted; `m.u` is retained for the metrics-staleness display (AC5). The frontend poll-driven stop + active-session guard (AC7) is unchanged - it now fires on an authoritative `stopped` rather than a guess.
- [REQ-VAULT-016](vault.md#req-vault-016-vault-graph-extraction-emits-the-canonical-shared-schema) added (extraction output-shape contract, split out of [REQ-VAULT-003](vault.md#req-vault-003-user-curated-edits-are-detected-and-ingested-within-60s) so detection latency and graph-output shape are separate REQs): Pi vault-graph extraction is brought up to Claude parity for text/structural content. AC1 - the Pi deterministic baseline (`memory-vault.ts` -> new pure `deterministicVaultGraph` helper) and its vault-extract subagent now emit the canonical graphify schema (`file_type`/`source_file`/`relation`/`confidence`) shared with repo and global graphs, replacing the legacy `type`/`path`/`mentions` shape; the prior shape gave nodes no `source_file`, so `graphify global add` label-merged every Pi node (documents included), collapsing their identity in the unified graph. The baseline now also emits a sub-section node per markdown heading (level 2+) with a `contains` edge, and the subagent layers `code` nodes, prose-concept nodes (deduped against baseline wikilink concepts by label), `conceptually_related_to`/`references` edges, and a confidence rubric. AC2 - the viz publish step (`graphify cluster-only .` -> copy `graph.html` to `Raw/Graphs/vault-graph.html`) is codified. The sibling Pi memory-capture prompt ([REQ-MEM-001](memory.md#req-mem-001-conversation-context-automatically-captured-to-vault) `memory-agent-prompt.md`), which writes session-note graph fragments into the same `user_vault` graph, is aligned to the same canonical schema so `graph.json` is no longer a mix of canonical and legacy nodes - it previously emitted the legacy `type`/`mentions`/`related` shape while Claude's memory-capture already emitted canonical. PDF text-layer ingestion for Pi remains out of scope (the Pi Read tool does not render PDF pages, unlike the Claude runtime; scanned/image PDFs are inherently impossible on Pi) and is tracked under [REQ-VAULT-011](vault.md#req-vault-011-vault-extract-ingests-pdf-files), whose `@impl` stays Claude-only.
- [REQ-AGENT-023](agents.md#req-agent-023-knowledge-graph-capability-graphify) / [REQ-AGENT-043](agents.md#req-agent-043-graphify-build-mode-dispatch): Pi graphify preseed now includes an Architecture graph option, a no-graph escape option, and a corrected Full semantic merge path. `build-graphify-architecture.sh` creates scoped file/module dependency graphs by filtering tests/docs/generated/config noise and projecting Graphify's symbol graph; Full semantic merge now starts from a freshly recreated AST-only baseline and no longer passes semantic sources as `prune_sources`, because Graphify prunes after adding and would delete the semantic nodes just merged. The Pi manifest and generated agent seed include the architecture script, and tests assert the script is preseeded advanced-only.
- [REQ-AGENT-023](agents.md#req-agent-023-knowledge-graph-capability-graphify) / [REQ-AGENT-025](agents.md#req-agent-025-post-clone-graph-triage) / [REQ-AGENT-043](agents.md#req-agent-043-graphify-build-mode-dispatch): Pi graphify now follows official Graphify flows for AST/build/cache/cluster/report/export output while keeping labels local to the active agent session. The bounded Pi update wrapper is a thin safety wrapper around upstream `graphify update`; Pi first-build AST uses Graphify's own detect/extract/build/cluster/report/export modules without Codeflare-specific file allowlists or import rewrites; Full mode has Pi Agent subagents write semantic chunks into Graphify's cache/local fragment. The Pi main session writes `.graphify_labels.json`, then local Graphify module calls regenerate report/html from existing graph community assignments; `graphify label` and provider `--backend` flags are forbidden in the Pi workflow. Final `graphify-out/graph.html` and `graphify-out/callflow.html` are generated after labels are applied, and durable graph commits include both. Clone triage is simplified to a YES/NO graph-build prompt for missing graphs, with AST-only vs Full selection deferred to the graphify skill after detection. The Docker image omits Graphify provider extras such as Gemini.

## 2026-06-01

- [REQ-AGENT-036](agents.md#req-agent-036-pr-boundary-review-trigger-conditions): Pi no longer creates a PR-boundary review window from passive lifecycle events such as opening a repo, switching branches, reloading Pi, or ending a normal assistant turn. Existing protected-base PRs are enforced only after explicit head-moving PR-boundary commands (`git push`, `gh pr create`, `gh pr update-branch`, `gh repo sync`, merge) or when already-persisted pending review state exists.
- [REQ-AGENT-024](agents.md#req-agent-024-advanced-session-mode-graph-first-discipline) / [REQ-AGENT-026](agents.md#req-agent-026-knowledge-graph-persistence-via-git) / [REQ-AGENT-043](agents.md#req-agent-043-graphify-build-mode-dispatch): Pi graphify advanced-mode workflow now distinguishes first build from update. Missing graphs use `build-graphify-ast.sh` (local AST initial build), existing graphs use `safe-graphify-update.sh` (bounded `graphify update` refresh), and Full mode uses Pi `Agent` semantic subagents without a model override so they inherit the current main-session model. The Pi graphify skill also mirrors Claude's repo-persistence contract: remove blanket `graphify-out/` ignores, ignore only caches/intermediates, add `graphify-out/graph.json merge=graphify`, and commit durable graph outputs when push permission exists.
- [REQ-VAULT-013](vault.md#req-vault-013-silverbullet-subpath-adapter) AC5/AC7 reworded + AC8 added; [REQ-VAULT-008](vault.md#req-vault-008-zero-ui-vault-encryption) demoted Implemented -> Partial (AD69 fix for codeflare#445). The vault proxy now serves SilverBullet's native service worker for the `service_worker.js` registration fetch, REPLACING the key-shim that disabled the editor's persistent `sb_files_*` local-sync store and forced a full re-index on every cold load. The upstream worker bytes are stored verbatim and SHA-256 drift-guarded (`VAULT_NATIVE_SW_VERBATIM` in `src/routes/vault-native-sw.ts`); the SERVED worker applies `graftVaultKeyRecovery`, a deterministic transform that injects a `__cfRecover()` helper (re-fetch the key from the auth-gated `/.vault-key` endpoint when the in-memory key is empty) and calls it at the worker's two key-empty checkpoints. The graft is mandatory ([REQ-VAULT-008](vault.md#req-vault-008-zero-ui-vault-encryption) AC7): the native worker flushes its key 5s after the last client disconnects and loses it on idle-termination, so it has no key by the time the shell boots and SB bounces to `.auth` ("Authentication not enabled") even on cold boot. The integration deploys localized the trigger: deploy 1 (no graft) bounced; deploy 2 (graft on `get-encryption-key` only) still bounced, because the actual failure is the `config` message handler's `enableClientEncryption && !y` auth-gate, which reads the key directly and never asks `get-encryption-key`; deploy 3 grafts both sites. New AC8 (REQ-VAULT-013): the shell-path bootstrap-hop 302 is suppressed for Service-Worker-context fetches (`Sec-Fetch-Mode` present and != `navigate`) so the native worker's `cache.addAll` precache resolves against the real shell instead of a redirect that would hang the SW install; navigations and headerless clients still get the hop (fail-safe). The `/.client/*` precache-auth exemption (reserved REQ-VAULT-013 AC9) is NOT needed - the deploy showed `cache.addAll` resolves, so the precache fetches carry the cookie. Decision recorded in [AD69](../../documentation/decisions/README.md). Verified end-to-end on the integration deploy (mobile, 2026-06-01): cold boot reaches the editor with no `.auth` bounce, the console logs "Recovered encryption key from codeflare", `sb_files_*` is created, and the sync engine runs incremental 0-operation cycles. Final statuses: REQ-VAULT-008 returns to Implemented (it was demoted to Partial on 2026-05-31 while the graft was in flight) and REQ-VAULT-013 moves to Implemented for the first time. The retired key-shim (`VAULT_KEY_SHIM_SERVICE_WORKER_JS`) and its tests are removed.
- [REQ-AGENT-006](agents.md#req-agent-006-preseed-configs-generated-from-single-source-of-truth) AC6 / [REQ-AGENT-007](agents.md#req-agent-007-multi-agent-adaptation-pipeline) AC3 corrected: restored the Antigravity (`agy`) preseed adaptation lane. The 2026-05-30 Gemini->Antigravity migration removed the generator's `gemini` lane on the incorrect premise that agy has no rules/skills/agents directory convention; in fact agy reads the Gemini CLI global config tree, which Google's migration guidance confirms stays current (`~/.gemini/GEMINI.md` auto-loads across all workspaces and `~/.gemini/skills/` auto-loads; only per-workspace `.gemini` -> `.agents` changed, and codeflare seeds the home directory). The generator now emits an `antigravity` lane into `~/.gemini/`: rules concatenated into `GEMINI.md`, skills into `skills/`, subagents into `agents/`, with Claude tool names remapped to the Gemini CLI vocabulary (`read_file`, `write_file`, `replace`, `run_shell_command`, `search_file_content`, `glob`). The prior Constraint claiming the generator "emits nothing" for Antigravity was false (the lane's `.gemini/` output had been silently relied on via bisynced R2 artifacts) and is replaced. `agent-seed-manifest.test.ts` gains lane-presence, both-skills-and-agents, and tool-remap/path-rewrite assertions. `entrypoint.sh` bisync filters now exclude the agy CLI runtime churn under `~/.gemini/antigravity-cli/` (binary, conversation recordings, brain/cache/log, updater - ~33MB of regenerable or conflict-prone data), matching the existing `.claude`/`.codex`/`.copilot` exclusion policy; the seeded `~/.gemini/` config and the root auth files still sync so agy auth persists across sessions like every other agent.

## 2026-05-31

- [REQ-AUTH-019](authentication.md#req-auth-019-user-identity-and-account-status-api) added (Implemented): documents the signed-in user's identity and account-status API - the authoritative `GET /api/user` read, the onboarding-complete marker, and the R2 scoped-token status and ensure endpoints - now covered by automated route tests.
- [REQ-SESSION-017](session-lifecycle.md#req-session-017-container-health-and-startup-status-api) added (Implemented): documents the container health check and the non-blocking startup-status polling endpoint whose reported stage tracks real container state through to ready, now covered by automated route tests.
- REQ-AGENT-016 (consult-llm preference toggle) removed. The explicit Settings toggle was never built and is not planned; the multi-model consultation feature stays implicitly active whenever a provider key is present. Moved to the agents domain Out of Scope.
- [REQ-VAULT-013](vault.md#req-vault-013-silverbullet-subpath-adapter) auto-demoted Implemented to Partial: the served shim service worker disables the editor's client-side file-sync cache, so the editor re-indexes its local store repeatedly within a session (open bug codeflare#445). AC5-AC7 are not fully correct until that regression is fixed.
- REQ-AGENT-042 (Graphify Hard-Block Enforcement) removed. The hard-block originated as [REQ-AGENT-024](agents.md#req-agent-024-advanced-session-mode-graph-first-discipline) AC5, was later split into its own REQ-AGENT-042, and is now retired entirely (this supersedes the older AC5-era entries below); graph-first discipline is advisory only going forward (the preseeded `graph-first` rule plus the per-call soft nudge in [REQ-AGENT-024](agents.md#req-agent-024-advanced-session-mode-graph-first-discipline)). The Claude PreToolUse hard-block hook (`enforce-graphify.sh`) and the equivalent structural-search gate in Pi `codeflare-pi.ts` are removed, along with the `/tmp/graphify-bypass` sentinel, after the count-based block proved to misfire on legitimate single-file searches that the graph-first rule itself excludes.
- [REQ-AGENT-041](agents.md#req-agent-041-pr-boundary-review-bypass-surfaces) / [REQ-AGENT-059](agents.md#req-agent-059-pi-durable-review-fix-loop): Pi's review-bypass sentinel now consumes once but acknowledges the current protected PR HEAD so same-head catch-up enforcement cannot respawn reviewers after the user explicitly bypasses; Claude keeps its existing one-turn Stop-hook sentinel behavior without advancing the ack checkpoint. Pi checks pending review freshness before consuming the sentinel: stale pending state is discarded without consuming it, and an advanced pending window acknowledges the live PR head rather than the superseded head. Pi review autofix remains automatic by default, but if the latest explicit user directive says not to automatically fix/implement or to wait for approval, the hidden follow-up is suppressed and the visible findings wait for the user's GO.
- [REQ-AGENT-040](agents.md#req-agent-040-pr-boundary-lane-classification-and-agent-dispatch) AC6/AC7: Claude Stop-hook in-flight suppression now treats a current-head Agent spawn whose completion marker falls past the transcript recency bound as orphaned, so the lane is demanded again instead of satisfying `spawned_after_push` forever. Final acknowledgement remains stricter than demand suppression: every required lane must have a current-head completion marker before `.git/sdd-last-ack-pr-head` advances.
- [REQ-AGENT-036](agents.md#req-agent-036-pr-boundary-review-trigger-conditions) / [REQ-AGENT-040](agents.md#req-agent-040-pr-boundary-lane-classification-and-agent-dispatch) / [REQ-AGENT-055](agents.md#req-agent-055-pi-pr-boundary-review-window-advancement) Pi PR-boundary review enforcement now treats a descendant PR-head change during an in-flight review as an advanced review window, resets per-head breaker state when rolling forward, preserves the first unreviewed base, keeps earlier result artifacts for audit, and rejects remote-tracking reflog bases unless backed by an ack or completed previous review. `gh pr create` metadata-lag handling now infers only `main`/`master` (including quoted base values, or the protected default when no base is supplied) before synthesizing a local-HEAD PR, so integration-branch PR creates stay deferred.
- [REQ-AGENT-005](agents.md#req-agent-005-pro-mode-includes-additional-skills-rules-agents-and-mcp-servers) AC2 corrected: Pro-mode persistent memory is delivered by syncing the user's Vault directory tree to their R2 bucket, not by a `.memory/` directory; the legacy `.memory/` tree is no longer written. Standard mode excludes the Vault tree so memory does not persist across container restarts.
- [REQ-SUB-019](subscription.md#req-sub-019-session-limit-popup-in-frontend) AC1/AC2 corrected: at the tier session cap the "New Session" control stays enabled but opens a limit popup instead of starting a session. The popup shows the running-session count and a progress bar with a dismiss control, rather than listing sessions with per-session stop controls.
- [REQ-TERM-007](terminal.md#req-term-007-tiling-layouts-2-split-3-split-4-grid) AC4 corrected: adding a terminal tab beyond the current layout's pane count downgrades the layout to tabbed rather than auto-upgrading to a larger tiling layout.
- [REQ-SESSION-010](session-lifecycle.md#req-session-010-session-status-observable-from-dashboard) AC7 corrected: when polling stops a session its terminal connections are disposed, but the currently active session is exempt from this poll-driven stop and is not cleared.
- [REQ-SETUP-010](setup.md#req-setup-010-social-share-preview-metadata-on-the-public-landing-page) AC4 corrected: the page meta description extends the `og:description` (same tagline plus a short product descriptor) rather than matching it exactly.
- [REQ-SETUP-009](setup.md#req-setup-009-subscribe-page-with-tier-selection) AC2 corrected: the subscribe flow is a two-phase wizard (overview, then tier selection); checkout is an external payment-provider handoff, not an internal phase.
- [REQ-SUB-006](subscription.md#req-sub-006-real-time-usage-tracking-via-timekeeper-do) AC6 corrected: the usage-flush handler retries failed durable-storage writes on a fixed 30-second interval rather than exponential backoff.

## 2026-05-30

- [REQ-MEM-001](memory.md#req-mem-001-conversation-context-automatically-captured-to-vault) / [REQ-MEM-002](memory.md#req-mem-002-capture-triggers-every-15-user-messages) / [REQ-VAULT-003](vault.md#req-vault-003-user-curated-edits-are-detected-and-ingested-within-60s) Pi parity fix: Pi memory capture now mirrors Claude's counter semantics by counting real user prompts from the durable transcript plus the submitted prompt, excluding synthetic `<task-notification>` / command-wrapper user records, baselining brand-new sessions, force-firing resumed-session capture when `/tmp` has no counter and the transcript already has more than one real user prompt, and triggering routine capture when the delta since the last capture reaches 15. Pi Vault indexing now shares Claude's `vault-extract.last` mtime high-water marker and exclusions (`Raw/Sessions/`, `graphify-out/`, `.silverbullet/`, and the four preseed root pages), so restored Vault content and memory-capture notes do not spawn the Vault indexing agent; only user-curated Vault changes do.
- [REQ-AGENT-052](agents.md#req-agent-052-pi-commit-attribution-and-local-build-hook-hardening) AC2 reworded: the attribution guard (`block-attributed-commits.sh` and the mirrored `codeflare-pi.ts` `ensureNoAttributedCommit`) now matches genuine attribution signatures only (Co-Authored-By, bot noreply email, generated-with footer, attribution emoji) and no longer matches bare model/product names (`claude code`, `claude opus`, etc.). Those tokens false-positived on legitimate prose (a PR titled "Claude Code parity" was blocked) and on git/gh commands naming `preseed/agents/claude/` paths. The Constraint now records that the Pi guard is a deliberate superset (it also matches the brain emoji and `ChatGPT`, since a Pi session may run a non-Claude model).
- [REQ-AGENT-013](agents.md#req-agent-013-browser-shim-for-oauth-flows) AC4 expanded to specify multi-row URL assembly. Terminal auth-URL detection now joins soft-wrap and application-newline continuation rows to the end of the terminal buffer instead of stopping at the visible viewport, fixing truncation of long OAuth URLs on narrow or mobile-keyboard-shrunk viewports (a real Antigravity Google sign-in failure: the truncated URL was rejected by Google with `invalid_scope`). The per-logical-line join is bounded by a fixed cap (`MAX_URL_CONTINUATION_ROWS`) so the periodic buffer scan cannot walk an unbounded scrollback. AC4 text appended (not replaced); `@impl` added for `web-ui/src/stores/terminal-url-detection.ts`; `@test` added for the new behavioural test. The New Session dialog agent list was also reordered to alphabetical by display label with Bash pinned last (no REQ governs display order; behaviour is now test-guarded).
- Added a Pi `startup-header` extension (Pi runtime, default and advanced modes): replaces Pi's built-in startup header with a boxed header showing model, thinking effort, context usage, active/total tool counts, cwd, and session file, with a `/builtin-header` command to restore the default. Self-contained cosmetic capability.
- Bumped graphify 0.8.18 -> 0.8.25 and added a `graphify` job to the shadow-pin sweep ([REQ-OPS-020](operations.md#req-ops-020-shadow-pin-version-bump-automation)). The graphifyy PyPI pin lives in `preseed/agents/claude/plugins/graphify/.claude-plugin/plugin.json` (the Dockerfile reads it via `jq`), so it was invisible to both Dependabot and the existing bump-shadow-pins jobs. [REQ-OPS-020](operations.md#req-ops-020-shadow-pin-version-bump-automation) AC2 now names graphifyy as a watched PyPI package alongside the context-mode npm watch, and the workflow-files test asserts the new job. The 0.8.25 release fixes the phantom-god-node and built-in-globals graph-pollution classes relevant to codeflare's graph quality.
- consult-llm skill raised to v2.1.0 with two new agent-behaviour ACs on [REQ-AGENT-031](agents.md#req-agent-031-consult-llm-key-isolation-subscription-backend-and-multi-agent-parity) (Status -> Partial). AC4: when the user does not name a provider, the agent must show an interactive provider-selection dialog (multi-select over OpenAI and Google Gemini) instead of silently defaulting. AC5: the agent always passes an explicit `model` resolved live to the provider's current latest flagship (OpenAI `/v1/models`, Gemini `/v1beta/models`), never the MCP server's static default, with an explicitly named model overriding the auto-pick. Both ACs are skill-directed behaviour with no automated test, hence Partial.
- PR-boundary review dispatch made non-blocking and re-summon-safe ([REQ-AGENT-040](agents.md#req-agent-040-pr-boundary-lane-classification-and-agent-dispatch) AC6/AC7). Review agents are now dispatched with `run_in_background: true` so the main session stays interactive, and the Stop hook (`enforce-review-spawn.sh`) gained an in-flight guard: when a required lane is spawned-but-not-yet-completed it exits 0 (without advancing the ack pointer) instead of demanding a fresh wave, fixing a re-summon loop that fired when a push landed while the prior wave was still running. A paired behavioural rule in `rules/git-workflow.md` forbids pushing or starting a second wave while one is in flight. The in-flight tolerance is bounded by transcript recency (`IN_FLIGHT_STALE_LINES`): an uncompleted spawn that falls far behind the transcript tail is treated as orphaned (crashed/killed subagent) and enforcement re-fires, so a dead lane cannot suppress the gate indefinitely.
- Removed the context-mode `enforce-ctx-mode.sh` Bash/WebFetch/Grep deny-gate ([REQ-AGENT-027](agents.md#req-agent-027-context-mode-interoperability)). The gate forced every shell command through `ctx_execute` and caused cascading "Cancelled: parallel tool call" failures; context-mode stays as a tool (MCP server plus the indexing PreToolUse/PostToolUse/PreCompact/SessionStart hooks), only the deny-gate is gone. [REQ-AGENT-027](agents.md#req-agent-027-context-mode-interoperability) AC1 was rewritten (graphify now runs unimpeded with no whitelist needed; stale gates are stripped on boot by the managed-hooks prune regex) and dropped to Status: Partial since AC1 no longer has a dedicated automated test. The obsolete gate tests `host/__tests__/enforce-ctx-mode.test.js` and `host/__tests__/enforce-ctx-mode-graphify.test.js` were removed (both spawned the deleted hook script and failed with ENOENT in CI); the settings.json hook-merge dedup/prune coverage in `entrypoint-enforce-ctx-mode-dedup.test.js` is retained.
- Replaced the Gemini CLI agent with the Antigravity CLI agent and adjusted the beta-badge roster ([REQ-AGENT-001](agents.md#req-agent-001-support-multiple-ai-coding-agents), [REQ-AGENT-002](agents.md#req-agent-002-agent-selection-at-session-creation), [REQ-TERM-005](terminal.md#req-term-005-tab-1-auto-starts-the-configured-agent)). The launchable `gemini` agent type was removed from the seven-agent roster and Antigravity put in its place: Antigravity is `agy`, a Go-native binary installed via `curl -fsSL https://antigravity.google/cli/install.sh | bash`, launched with `agy --dangerously-skip-permissions`, and (like OpenCode) excluded from the npm agent-install line and the V8 compile-cache warmup. The Gemini API integration that backs consult-llm is unchanged: GEMINI_API_KEY injection, the LLM Keys settings UI, and [REQ-AGENT-020](agents.md#req-agent-020-llm-api-key-management-ui) all remain intact (only the CLI agent was removed, not the API provider). In the UI, Antigravity carries a beta badge while copilot and pi were promoted out of beta. Net agent count stays seven (claude-code, codex, copilot, antigravity, opencode, pi, bash). [REQ-TERM-005](terminal.md#req-term-005-tab-1-auto-starts-the-configured-agent) AC3's tab-1 agent-launch list was updated from Gemini to Antigravity and completed to include Pi plus the no-agent bash fallback.
- [REQ-AGENT-060](agents.md#req-agent-060-pi-durable-review-lane-tool-surface) added: Pi durable PR-boundary review lanes now additively load graphify and settings-enabled context-mode while keeping recursive review enforcement and `@gotgenes/pi-subagents` out of the lane process. Also consolidated the triplicated `reviewResultPath`/`reviewResultsDir` into a single `review-jobs.ts` source and removed dead pre-durable spawn helpers (`startReviewLaneSpawns`, `isReviewCompletionForLane`, `isCurrentReviewHead`).
- [REQ-MEM-001](memory.md#req-mem-001-conversation-context-automatically-captured-to-vault) AC8 added: memory capture now reads the durable on-disk session transcript instead of a volatile in-memory buffer. Pi's `memory-vault.ts` was building the capture from a module-level `lastMessages` array populated only on `agent_end`, so the first capture after any Pi reload/resume saw an empty buffer and wrote a hollow "no substantive content in range" note even though Pi's full session JSONL (the same file `/resume` reads) sat on disk. It now reads `ctx.sessionManager.getSessionFile()` and parses it via the new `parseSessionMessages` helper, with a skip-empty guard that suppresses the capture entirely when the resolved transcript is blank. The Claude capture subagent (`memory-capture.md`) additionally gains the context-mode execute tools alongside Bash so its prefilter/merge pipeline runs whether or not a shell-routing gate is active.
- [REQ-AGENT-040](agents.md#req-agent-040-pr-boundary-lane-classification-and-agent-dispatch) AC6/AC7 in-flight guard fixed from blanket to per-lane suppression. The first cut exited 0 for the WHOLE Stop-hook gate whenever any one required lane was in flight; with a long-running code-reviewer that masked the entire gate every turn, so the sequential doc-updater demand never fired even after spec-reviewer completed (doc-updater was silently skipped across a full PR review). The gate now guards each lane independently (`! spawned_after_push <lane> && ! lane_in_flight <lane>`), keeping the re-summon-loop fix while letting the sequential/independent doc-updater lane be demanded on schedule. Behavioral hook tests in `host/__tests__/enforce-review-spawn.test.js` cover per-lane suppression, stale-orphan re-demand, and no ack for a pre-push in-flight lane without current-head coverage. Also resolved the doc-updater drift findings from this PR's review: `documentation/lanes/preseed.md` (codeflare-hooks dispatch is non-blocking background, and the context-mode Bash deny-gate was removed), `documentation/lanes/ci-cd.md` (bump-shadow-pins now watches the graphifyy PyPI pin), and `documentation/lanes/container.md` (consult-llm provider AskUserQuestion dialog + latest-flagship model resolution).
- [REQ-AGENT-031](agents.md#req-agent-031-consult-llm-key-isolation-subscription-backend-and-multi-agent-parity) (AC4/AC5) and [REQ-AGENT-027](agents.md#req-agent-027-context-mode-interoperability) (AC1) lifted from Partial to Implemented. The earlier same-day entries above called these skill-directed/AC1 behaviours untested; they are now verified by content assertions over the bundled agent seed in `src/__tests__/lib/agent-seed-manifest.test.ts` (the same pattern used for the shadow-pin and Pi-script seed tests): [REQ-AGENT-031](agents.md#req-agent-031-consult-llm-key-isolation-subscription-backend-and-multi-agent-parity) asserts the consult-llm SKILL.md mandates the AskUserQuestion provider dialog when no provider is named and an explicit latest-flagship model resolved live (`/v1/models`, `/v1beta/models`) rather than the MCP server default; [REQ-AGENT-027](agents.md#req-agent-027-context-mode-interoperability) asserts no `enforce-ctx-mode` deny-gate is preseeded in any seeded config. [REQ-AGENT-040](agents.md#req-agent-040-pr-boundary-lane-classification-and-agent-dispatch) AC6/AC7 (background dispatch + bounded in-flight guard) gains behavioral coverage that runs `enforce-review-spawn.sh` against fresh and stale in-flight lane fixtures.

This keeps merge enforcement recoverable across reloads and independent of ephemeral Agent IDs.

This keeps the commands working both with context-mode disabled and after `/ctx on` reloads Pi resources.
- [REQ-AGENT-040](agents.md#req-agent-040-pr-boundary-lane-classification-and-agent-dispatch) updated: Pi PR-boundary review dispatch now starts reviewers directly from the extension, records registered subagent IDs, dedupes paired Pi tool-result events, and scopes follow-up push reviews to the unreviewed incremental diff. Prompt-based reviewer launch instructions were removed so PR-boundary enforcement no longer depends on the assistant manually calling `Agent`.
- [REQ-AGENT-021](agents.md#req-agent-021-pro-mode-sdd-workflow-preseed-and-tool-surface-portability) AC5 updated: CI monitoring keeps the existing single tail-followed native-Bash monitor, but launches it in a background task/subagent so the main session remains usable while CI runs; agents still must retrieve the terminal `CI_RESULT success` before claiming green or deploying.
- [REQ-AGENT-023](agents.md#req-agent-023-knowledge-graph-capability-graphify) AC4/AC5 updated: Pi's graphify surface is now active-repo and branch aware when the packaged native tools resolve the session cwd (`/home/user/workspace`) instead of the checked-out repo. `codeflare-pi.ts` tracks command-local `cd ... &&` and `git -C ...` forms, injects `<repo>:<branch>@<head>` into session context, and retries `graphify_query` / `graphify_path` / `graphify_explain` against `<active-repo>/graphify-out/graph.json` via `--graph` when the first native call reports the missing workspace-root graph.
- [REQ-AGENT-005](agents.md#req-agent-005-pro-mode-includes-additional-skills-rules-agents-and-mcp-servers) AC4 updated: Pi agents now declare the context-mode helper tools (`ctx_execute`, `ctx_batch_execute`, `ctx_execute_file`, `ctx_search`, `ctx_fetch_and_index`) in their frontmatter instead of having them stripped. The shared Claude agent definitions are remapped to Pi-native tool names in `generate-agent-seed.mjs` (TOOL_MAP.pi + the Pi allowlist) and the deploy-time strip in `r2-seed.ts` was removed. The declarations are inert when context-mode is disabled (the tools do not exist so Pi drops them) and usable when `/ctx on` enables it, closing the dead-end where an agent could be told to route to a ctx tool it did not have. No Pi-specific agent variants; Pi stays fully functional with context-mode off.
- Pi review-enforcement and context-mode decoupling (no REQ behavior change; both behavior-preserving for users): the PR-boundary review circuit breaker now latches to stop the unbounded reminder/respawn spiral, the subagents service is only seeded with a real session ctx, and the always-excluded local context-mode enforcement extensions were deleted with shell-command detection switched from ctx_* tool-name matching to command-content matching so the extensions run identically with context-mode off or on.
- [REQ-AGENT-050](agents.md#req-agent-050-pi-native-review-workflow-skill) added: Pi-native `/review` workflow skill. Because Claude slash commands do not deploy to Pi, the Pi `/review` command now injects a dedicated Pi-native `review` skill that mirrors the Claude `commands/review.md` multi-perspective workflow, instead of the `git-review-pipeline` enforcement skill. [REQ-AGENT-015](agents.md#req-agent-015-review-command-for-multi-perspective-codebase-review) cross-references the Pi delivery and gains the Pi skill/command `@impl` anchors; [REQ-AGENT-007](agents.md#req-agent-007-multi-agent-adaptation-pipeline)'s Pi native-runtime-exception clause now covers native command handlers and Pi-native skills.
- [REQ-AGENT-051](agents.md#req-agent-051-pi-debug-deploy-and-brainstorm-commands) added: Pi `/debug`, `/deploy`, and `/brainstorm` commands. These workflows ship as Claude slash commands that do not deploy to Pi, so a Pi extension reimplements them as native `pi.registerCommand` handlers that inject the adapted workflow text.
- [REQ-AGENT-052](agents.md#req-agent-052-pi-commit-attribution-and-local-build-hook-hardening) added: Pi commit-attribution and local-build hook hardening. The attribution guard widened to `gh pr/issue/release` and `git merge/tag/notes`, the detection set aligned to the canonical `block-attributed-commits.sh` (including `noreply@anthropic` and model-name variants) with the bare-"Claude" false-positive removed, and the local-build guard gained `oxlint`/`prettier` plus a user-only consume-on-use `/tmp/local-build-bypass` sentinel.
- [REQ-MEM-014](memory.md#req-mem-014-pi-capture-contract-transcript-prefilter-and-model-fidelity-lever) added: Pi capture contract, transcript prefilter, and model-fidelity lever ([AD58](../../documentation/decisions/README.md#ad58-sonnet-for-memory-capture-with-prefilter-and-scratchpad) parity). Pi now ships full capture-contract and vault-extract prompt files via the manifest to `~/.pi/agent/prompts/` (replacing the thin inline contract), the transcript is prefiltered to user/assistant text only before capture (last 200 turns, 8000 chars/turn) instead of a raw last-40-message slice, and the capture/extract spawn reads an optional model from `CODEFLARE_MEMORY_MODEL` with no hardcoded model name. [REQ-MEM-001](memory.md#req-mem-001-conversation-context-automatically-captured-to-vault) and [REQ-MEM-008](memory.md#req-mem-008-memory-prompt-files-preseeded-via-manifest-pipeline) gained the Pi prompt/helpers `@impl` anchors.
- [REQ-AGENT-023](agents.md#req-agent-023-knowledge-graph-capability-graphify) updated: the Pi-owned graphify wrapper now fails closed (aborts when the target directory is missing, the RLIMIT_AS cap cannot apply, or the `graphify` CLI is absent) and always re-exports `GRAPHIFY_VIZ_NODE_LIMIT`; the Pi session-start graph summary skips the synchronous parse on graphs over 30MB, bounds its git probes with a timeout, and keeps the structural-search gate fail-open.

## 2026-05-24

- Round-4: **[REQ-MEM-002](memory.md#req-mem-002-capture-triggers-every-15-user-messages) AC6 redesigned around `/tmp` ephemerality** (Cloudflare Containers contract; cf. `~/Vault/References/Cloudflare-Containers-Ephemerality.md`). Round-3 shipped a `RESUME_GAP_SEC > 1800` mtime heuristic for resume detection, which all three review agents flagged as untestable and which the user immediately falsified ("5-min resumes happen regularly"). The fix moves the per-session counter from `$HOME/.memory/counter/` (bisync'd to R2, survives recycle) to `/tmp/.memory-counter/` (ephemeral by platform contract, guaranteed empty on every container start). The counter's absence on first hook fire is now the canonical "fresh container instance" signal. Brand-new vs. resumed is distinguished by transcript content (`CURRENT_COUNT == 1` vs `> 1`); on resume, capture force-fires from line 1 to flush any prior-session tail, and the graph-query directive is re-emitted because the agent's in-context recall is gone after recycle. AC6 rewritten, AC1 + AC2 + AC3 updated to reference the new gating. Companion `memory-capture-block.sh` PreToolUse hook updated to read from the new counter location (silent gate-failure prevented). `entrypoint.sh` bisync filter `--filter "- .memory/counter/**"` and the boot-time `mkdir -p ~/.memory/counter` removed (both obsolete). `documentation/lanes/memory.md` Hook Mechanics + Counter Storage + Troubleshooting sections rewritten; `documentation/lanes/storage-and-sync.md` always-exclude list updated. Three real behavioural tests added covering AC6: resumed-session force-fire from line 1, AC6 boundary case (`CURRENT_COUNT == 1` is brand-new not resume), and brand-new baseline path. Tests use `MEMCAP_COUNTER_DIR` env-var override for hermetic temp dirs (production never sets it). Vault note `~/Vault/References/Cloudflare-Containers-Ephemerality.md` captures the verified Cloudflare contract that this design rests on.

After a 2h idle stop + restart, the prior 3-minute give-up left users with a permanently disabled vault button if the container took longer than the budget to bind SilverBullet, with no recovery path short of stopping the session.

- Verification-label audit (60 Integration-test REQs with annotated test files). Following CQ-1 truth check, all 63 REQs labeled `Verification: Integration test` were cross-checked against unit-test files mentioning the REQ-ID. 60 had at least one mention. Per-REQ analysis of how many AC numbers are referenced inside those unit tests: 0 REQs have full AC-number coverage in unit tests, 6 have some AC numbers referenced but not all ([REQ-MEM-001](memory.md#req-mem-001-conversation-context-automatically-captured-to-vault) missing AC2/6/7, [REQ-MEM-004](memory.md#req-mem-004-vault-contents-synced-to-r2-across-sessions) missing AC2/3/4/6, [REQ-MEM-006](memory.md#req-mem-006-memory-available-only-in-pro-advanced-mode) missing AC1/2/4, [REQ-MEM-011](memory.md#req-mem-011-session-mode-storage-resolution-and-propagation) missing AC1/4, [REQ-SESSION-008](session-lifecycle.md#req-session-008-container-restart-preserves-r2-bucket) missing AC2-5, [REQ-STOR-003](storage.md#req-stor-003-bidirectional-sync-every-15-minutes-with-manual-triggers) missing AC2-4), 54 mention REQ-ID only as a cross-reference without per-AC verification. **All 60 REQs remain `Status=Implemented`. The audit checked whether unit-test references densely span every AC (signal that the unit test alone could authoritatively verify the REQ and the `Verification:` label could be relabelled to `Automated test`); they do not, so the existing `Integration test` label is correct. The audit did NOT and does not propose any Status downgrade - Integration tests are automated CI verifications, and a REQ with `Verification: Integration test` is fully `Implemented` once the integration test covers all ACs.** Recorded here so future passes do not re-derive.

## 2026-05-19

- [REQ-MEM-001](memory.md#req-mem-001-conversation-context-automatically-captured-to-vault) AC3 / [REQ-SESSION-016](session-lifecycle.md#req-session-016-user-timezone-propagated-from-preferences-to-container-env) wiring fix: `handleSetBucketName` (`src/container/index.ts`) was silently dropping `userTimezone` from the DO entry-point JSON destructure. The Worker forwarded the browser's IANA tz, but the DO never read the field, so `USER_TIMEZONE` was always empty inside containers and capture filenames fell through to UTC. Destructure restored; field now flows through `setBucketName` -> `applyBucketName` and through `applyPrefsOnRestart`. `applyPrefsOnRestart` userTimezone branch now persists-before-mutates (matches the `ensureVaultKey` precedent) and validates the IANA shape at the DO boundary so path-traversal / junk strings cannot reach storage or the entrypoint symlink. Semantics documented as "sticky once set": empty/undefined/malformed inputs are no-op, since the Worker filters empties upstream via the truthy spread in `buildSetBucketNameBody`. Regression coverage added at two layers: helper-level unit tests (`src/__tests__/container/container-env.test.ts`) and HTTP-level integration tests (`src/__tests__/container/index.test.ts`) that POST to `/_internal/setBucketName` and assert `USER_TIMEZONE` surfaces on `envVars`. The HTTP-level tests fail if the destructure is reverted, closing the test-theater gap left by the helper-only tests.
- Always-loaded preseed rules trimmed: `spec-discipline.md` (60->33 lines), `documentation-discipline.md` (41->19), `karpathy.md` (38->19), `tdd-discipline.md` (30->17). Net ~48% reduction on the affected rules with no behavioural drift.

Server-side merges into `develop` advance the develop->main PR HEAD without producing a local `git push` line in the session transcript; without this addition the review pipeline silently failed to arm after every feature-branch merge. Layer 2 (`gh pr view` authoritative PR HEAD SHA) continues to filter false positives.

- [REQ-AGENT-021](agents.md#req-agent-021-pro-mode-sdd-workflow-preseed-and-tool-surface-portability) AC22 added: Phase 5 enrichment now queries the project's `graphify-out/graph.json` via `mcp__graphify__get_neighbors` (cross-link Dependencies), `mcp__graphify__god_nodes` (ADR-seed candidates), and `mcp__graphify__query_graph` (glossary concept nodes). Tool-agnostic across Bash and context-mode surfaces.

## 2026-05-17
- [REQ-AGENT-024](agents.md#req-agent-024-advanced-session-mode-graph-first-discipline) gains AC6 (mandatory `AskUserQuestion` two-mode prompt before semantic-extraction subagent dispatch in `/graphify` builds, with subagent count + wall-time estimate; skipped only when the corpus contains zero docs/papers/images) and AC7 (Part B subagents dispatched with `model: "haiku"`; Sonnet escalation only on `--mode deep`, Opus never).
